           </div>
          </div> <p>This page enables <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Administrators" title="Wikipedia:Administrators"><b>administrators</b></a> to handle requests for permissions on the English Wikipedia. Administrators are able to modify account creator, autopatrolled, confirmed, file mover, extended confirmed, mass message sender, new page reviewer, page mover, pending changes reviewer, rollback, template editor rights and AutoWikiBrowser access. </p><p>Editors wishing to request a permission flag here should do so <a href="#Process">following the procedure below</a>. Editors requesting permissions are advised to periodically revisit the requests page, as notifications will not always be given after a decision is made. Editors should not expect their request to be answered right away and should remember to be patient when filing a request. To find out what permissions your account has, go to <a href="/wiki/Special:Preferences" title="Special:Preferences">Special:Preferences</a>, where your permissions are listed in the user profile tab under "Member of groups". </p><p>Requests for permissions are archived regularly; please see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Archive" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Archive">Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Archive</a> for an index of past requests. </p> </td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="plainlinks ombox ombox-notice" role="presentation">

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Permissions">Permissions</span></h2> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Handled_here">Handled here</span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="User_groups">User groups</span></h4> 
      <ul>
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Account_creator" title="Wikipedia:Account creator">Account creator</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Account_creator&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=account+creator">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Account_creator" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Account creator">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> The account creator flag is granted to users who are active in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Request_an_account/Guide" title="Wikipedia:Request an account/Guide">request an account process</a>. The flag removes the limit on the maximum number of new accounts that can be created in a 24 hour period. It also allows users to make accounts with names similar to other accounts. The account creator flag is only given to users who participate in the ACC process and may be removed without notice should a user's participation in the account creation process cease.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Autopatrolled" title="Wikipedia:Autopatrolled">Autopatrolled</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Autopatrolled&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=autopatrolled">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Autopatrolled" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Autopatrolled">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> The autopatrolled flag is granted to users who are active in the creation of new articles. This tool is granted so their creations are <a href="/wiki/Special:Log/patrol" title="Special:Log/patrol">auto patrolled</a> in <a href="/wiki/Special:NewPages" title="Special:NewPages">Special:NewPages</a>. Unlike other requests, any user may nominate an editor for Autopatrolled, even without that user's consent. A user who wishes to have this flag generally should have created at least 25 articles and must be trusted, experienced, and must have demonstrated they are familiar with Wikipedia's policies and guidelines, especially <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Biographies_of_living_persons" title="Wikipedia:Biographies of living persons">WP:BLP</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Notability" title="Wikipedia:Notability">Wikipedia:Notability</a>.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AutoWikiBrowser" title="Wikipedia:AutoWikiBrowser">AutoWikiBrowser</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/AutoWikiBrowser&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=autowikibrowser">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/AutoWikiBrowser" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/AutoWikiBrowser">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AutoWikiBrowser" title="Wikipedia:AutoWikiBrowser">AutoWikiBrowser</a> is a semi-automated <a href="/wiki/MediaWiki" title="MediaWiki">MediaWiki</a> editor for <a href="/wiki/Microsoft_Windows" title="Microsoft Windows">Microsoft Windows</a>, designed to make tedious repetitive tasks quicker and easier. It is essentially a browser that automatically opens up a new page when the last is saved. When set to do so, it suggests some changes (typically formatting) that are generally meant to be incidental to the main change. Please read the quick <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AutoWikiBrowser/CheckPage#Guide" title="Wikipedia:AutoWikiBrowser/CheckPage">guide</a> on the main page before requesting permission. This is not a true <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:User_access_levels" title="Wikipedia:User access levels">user right</a>, but access needs to be granted by administrators just like other permissions. If approved, your name will be added to the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AutoWikiBrowser/CheckPage" title="Wikipedia:AutoWikiBrowser/CheckPage">CheckPage</a>. Users with under 250 non-automated mainspace edits <i>or</i> 500 total mainspace edits are rarely approved. You will need to give a reason for wanting AWB access.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:User_access_levels#Confirmed_users" title="Wikipedia:User access levels">Confirmed</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Confirmed&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=confirmed">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Confirmed" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Confirmed">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> The confirmed flag may be granted to new users who have not yet hit the threshold for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:User_access_levels#Autoconfirmed_users" title="Wikipedia:User access levels">autoconfirmed</a> status. These are users who have not had both 10 edits and 4 days experience. People with this flag can <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:File_Upload_Wizard" title="Wikipedia:File Upload Wizard">upload</a> files and edit <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Protection_policy#Semi-protection" title="Wikipedia:Protection policy">semi-protected</a> pages before hitting the autoconfirmed flag. Users requesting this flag must indicate clearly why they should be exempted from the customary confirmation period.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Event_coordinator" title="Wikipedia:Event coordinator">Event coordinator</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Event_coordinator&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=event+coordinator">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Event_coordinator" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Event coordinator">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> The event coordinator user right allows editors to create multiple new accounts, and to temporarily confirm accounts so that they can create new articles.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:User_access_levels#Extended_confirmed_users" title="Wikipedia:User access levels">Extended confirmed</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Extended_confirmed&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=extended+confirmed">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Extended_confirmed" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Extended confirmed">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> The extended confirmed flag is normally automatically added to accounts after 500 edits and 30 days, but may be added to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Sock_puppetry#Legitimate_uses" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Sock puppetry">legitimate alternate accounts</a> of users that already have this access. The flag allows users to edit pages under <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Protection_policy#Arbitration_30.2F500_protection" title="Wikipedia:Protection policy">extended confirmed protection</a>.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:File_mover" title="Wikipedia:File mover">File mover</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/File_mover&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=file+mover">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/File_mover" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/File mover">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> The file mover user right is intended to allow users experienced in working with files to rename them, <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:File_mover" title="Wikipedia:File mover">subject to policy</a>, with the ease that autoconfirmed users already enjoy when renaming Wikipedia articles.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Mass_message_senders" title="Wikipedia:Mass message senders">Mass message sender</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Mass_message_sender&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=mass+message+sender">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Mass_message_sender" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Mass message sender">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> Mass message sender enables users to send messages to multiple users at once. This flag is given to users who have made <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Mass_message_senders#Requesting_a_mailing" title="Wikipedia:Mass message senders">requests for delivery</a> in the past, clearly showing an understanding of the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Mass_message_senders#Guidance_for_use" title="Wikipedia:Mass message senders">guidance for use</a>.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:New_pages_patrol/Reviewers" title="Wikipedia:New pages patrol/Reviewers">New page reviewer</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/New_page_reviewer&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=new+page+reviewer">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/New_page_reviewer" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/New page reviewer">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> The new page reviewer user right allows users to mark pages as <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Help:Patrolled_edit" class="extiw" title="meta:Help:Patrolled edit">patrolled</a> and use the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Page_Curation/Help" title="Wikipedia:Page Curation/Help">page curation toolbar</a>. At administrators' discretion, the right may be accorded on a time limited basis or indefinite.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Page_mover" title="Wikipedia:Page mover">Page mover</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Page_mover&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=page+mover">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Page_mover" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Page mover">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> The page mover user right allows users <b>experienced</b> in working with article names to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Moving_a_page" title="Wikipedia:Moving a page">move them</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Page_mover" title="Wikipedia:Page mover">subject to policy</a>, without leaving behind a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Redirect" title="Wikipedia:Redirect">redirect</a>. They may also move all <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Subpages" title="Wikipedia:Subpages">subpages</a> when moving the parent page(s). General guidelines include making 3,000 edits and 6 months of editing history. At administrators' discretion, the right may be accorded on a time limited basis or indefinite.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Reviewing_pending_changes" title="Wikipedia:Reviewing pending changes">Pending changes reviewer</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Pending_changes_reviewer&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=pending+changes+reviewer">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Pending_changes_reviewer" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Pending changes reviewer">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> The reviewer flag is granted to users who are experienced enough with Wikipedia editing and its policies for contributing to the process of reviewing articles placed under <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Pending_changes" title="Wikipedia:Pending changes">pending changes</a>.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Rollback" title="Wikipedia:Rollback">Rollback</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Rollback&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=rollback">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Rollback" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Rollback">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> Rollback enables users to remove <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Vandalism" title="Wikipedia:Vandalism">vandalism</a> much more quickly and efficiently than by <a href="/wiki/Help:Reverting#Undo" title="Help:Reverting">undoing</a> it. Users who do not demonstrate an understanding of what constitutes <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Cleaning_up_vandalism" title="Wikipedia:Cleaning up vandalism">capable vandalism fighting</a>, either because they have no or little history of doing so, or show a poor ability to discern between <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Assume_good_faith" title="Wikipedia:Assume good faith">good and bad faith</a> edits <b>will not be granted this right</b>. Also, it is unlikely that editors with under 200 mainspace edits will have their request granted. For a more detailed explanation of rollback and information about when it is appropriate to use the tool, see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Rollback" title="Wikipedia:Rollback">Wikipedia:Rollback</a>. For information about the technical details of the feature, see <a href="/wiki/Help:Reverting#Rollback" title="Help:Reverting">here</a>.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Template_editor" title="Wikipedia:Template editor">Template editor</a> <small>(<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Template_editor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Template_editor/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=template+editor">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Template_editor" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Template editor">view requests</a></span>)</small>:</b> The template editor flag allows users to edit protected templates and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Lua" title="Wikipedia:Lua">Lua modules</a>. General guidelines for granting include making at least 1,000 edits overall (with at least 150 to templates or modules), being a registered user for over a year, and having a record of successfully proposing significant edits to several protected templates. Users should demonstrate proficiency with template syntax and an understanding of the need for caution when editing heavily-used templates.</li>
      </ul> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Handled_elsewhere">Handled elsewhere</span></h3> 
      <p>Several permissions are requested and handled elsewhere: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Administrators" title="Wikipedia:Administrators">Administrator</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Bureaucrats" title="Wikipedia:Bureaucrats">bureaucrat</a> access:</b> Requests for administrator or bureaucrat access need to be posted at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_adminship" title="Wikipedia:Requests for adminship">requests for adminship</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_adminship#Current_nominations_for_bureaucratship" title="Wikipedia:Requests for adminship">requests for bureaucratship</a>, respectively.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Bots" title="Wikipedia:Bots">Bots</a>:</b> Request for bot flags should be made at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Bots/Requests_for_approval" title="Wikipedia:Bots/Requests for approval">Wikipedia:Bots/Requests for approval</a>.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Edit_filter" title="Wikipedia:Edit filter">Edit filter</a>:</b> Requests for access to the <b>edit filter manager</b> group and the <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Edit_filter_helper" title="Wikipedia:Edit filter helper">edit filter helper</a></b> group should be made at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Edit_filter_noticeboard" title="Wikipedia:Edit filter noticeboard">Wikipedia:Edit filter noticeboard</a>.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Interface_administrators" title="Wikipedia:Interface administrators">Interface administrator</a>:</b> Requests for interface administrator access should be made at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Bureaucrats%27_noticeboard" title="Wikipedia:Bureaucrats' noticeboard">Wikipedia:Bureaucrats' noticeboard</a>. Only current administrators may become interface administrators.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:IP_block_exemption" title="Wikipedia:IP block exemption">IP-block-exempt</a>:</b> While the IP-block-exempt right can be granted by administrators, this flag is not handled here. Requests for the IP-block exempt right should be submitted via the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Unblock_Ticket_Request_System" title="Wikipedia:Unblock Ticket Request System">Unblock Ticket Request System</a> or, if there are significant privacy concerns, email the checkuser team at <span class="nowrap">checkuser-en-wp<img alt="@" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/At_sign.svg/15px-At_sign.svg.png" decoding="async" title="@" width="15" height="15" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/At_sign.svg/23px-At_sign.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/At_sign.svg/30px-At_sign.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="145" data-file-height="145">wikipedia.org</span> or contact a CheckUser directly.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CheckUser" title="Wikipedia:CheckUser">Checkuser</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Oversight" title="Wikipedia:Oversight">Oversight</a>:</b> These rights are only granted by the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Arbitration_Committee" title="Wikipedia:Arbitration Committee">Arbitration Committee</a>, and only after strict scrutiny. More information can be found <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Arbitration_Committee/CheckUser_and_Oversight#Appointments" title="Wikipedia:Arbitration Committee/CheckUser and Oversight">here</a>.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Articles_for_creation/Participants" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Articles for creation/Participants">AfC reviewer</a>:</b> This access is granted by administrators at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:WikiProject_Articles_for_creation/Participants" title="Wikipedia talk:WikiProject Articles for creation/Participants">Wikipedia talk:WikiProject Articles for creation/Participants</a>.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:New_pages_patrol/Redirect_whitelist" title="Wikipedia talk:New pages patrol/Redirect whitelist">Redirect patrol whitelist</a>:</b> Addition to the whitelist is granted by administrators at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:New_pages_patrol/Redirect_whitelist" title="Wikipedia talk:New pages patrol/Redirect whitelist">Wikipedia talk:New pages patrol/Redirect whitelist</a>.</li> 
       <li><b><a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Stewards" class="extiw" title="meta:Stewards">Steward</a></b> permissions can only be granted in <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Stewards/Elections" class="extiw" title="meta:Stewards/Elections">yearly elections</a>, and are rarely given.</li> 
       <li><b>Global permissions</b> such as global renamer, sysop, IP block exempt, rollback, etc should be made at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Steward_requests/Global_permissions" class="extiw" title="meta:Steward requests/Global permissions">meta:Steward requests/Global permissions</a>.</li>
      </ul> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Removal_of_permissions">Removal of permissions</span></h2> 
      <p>If you wish to have any of <b>your</b> permission flags (except administrator) removed, you should <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Administrators%27_noticeboard" title="Wikipedia:Administrators' noticeboard">contact an administrator</a>. If you want <b>your</b> administrator flag removed, you should contact a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Bureaucrats%27_noticeboard" title="Wikipedia:Bureaucrats' noticeboard">bureaucrat</a>. </p>
      <p>This is <b>not</b> the place to request review of another user's rights. If you believe someone's actions merit removal of a permission flag, you should raise your concern at the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Administrators%27_noticeboard/Incidents" title="Wikipedia:Administrators' noticeboard/Incidents">incidents noticeboard</a>. </p>
      <p>The bureaucrat, checkuser, and oversight flags are removed at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Steward_requests/permissions#Removal_of_access" class="extiw" title="meta:Steward requests/permissions">meta:Steward requests/Permissions</a>. Stewards will typically not carry out such requests unless they are made on behalf of the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Arbitration_Committee" title="Wikipedia:Arbitration Committee">Arbitration Committee</a>, by a user who is requesting their own access be removed, or in cases of an emergency. </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Process">Process</span></h2> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Requestors">Requestors</span></h3> 
      <p><b>To make a request for a permission, click "add request" next to the appropriate header and fill in the reason for wanting permission.</b> </p>
      <p>Any editor may comment on requests for permission. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Administrators">Administrators</span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Full instructions at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Administrator_instructions" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Administrator instructions">Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Administrator instructions</a>
      </div> 
      <p>Administrators are permitted to grant account creator, autopatrolled, confirmed, event coordinator, file mover, mass message sender, page mover, pending changes reviewer, rollback and template editor flags to any user who meets the <a href="#Permissions">criteria explained above</a> and can be trusted not to abuse the tool(s). Administrators may either grant these permissions permanently or temporarily. For convenience, a <a href="/wiki/User:MusikBot" title="User:MusikBot">bot</a> will automatically comment with relevant data if the user does not meet <a href="/wiki/User:MusikBot/PermClerk#Configuration" title="User:MusikBot/PermClerk">configurable</a> qualifications. Even if the bot does not comment, administrators should review the user's contributions and logs to ensure the tools will be used appropriately and check for any indication of potential misuse. </p>
      <p>Once an administrator has granted a permission or decided to deny a request, they should add {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Done" title="Template:Done">done</a>}} or {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Not_done" title="Template:Not done">not done</a>}} respectively under the request with their comments. If a user already has the requested permission, or is autoconfirmed and requesting confirmed, {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Already_done" title="Template:Already done">already done</a>}} should be used. <i>N</i> hours after the last comment was made (as specified by the <a href="/wiki/User:MusikBot/PermClerk#Configuration" title="User:MusikBot/PermClerk">config</a>), the request will be archived automatically: approved requests will be placed <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Approved" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Approved">here</a>; declined requests will go <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Denied" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Denied">here</a>. See <a href="/wiki/User:MusikBot/PermClerk#Archiving" title="User:MusikBot/PermClerk">User:MusikBot/PermClerk#Archiving</a> for more information on archiving functionality. </p> 
      <div style="clear:both;"></div>

        I'm fairly active on Wikipedia and have been doing a significant amount of search-and-replace editing in <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Television" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Television">Wikipedia:WikiProject Television</a> (specifically, some of the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Television#Maintenance_categories" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Television">maintenance categories</a>), and now also in <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Westerns" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Westerns">Wikipedia:WikiProject Westerns</a>. AWB would assist in several of the more search-replace oriented elements (adding the project banner to genre categories, removal of obsolete and/or empty template parameters, proper formatting of dates, replacing invalid hex colors, adding categories, etc). I'm familiar with Wikipedia's guidelines and understand I am responsible for the edits done when using AWB. <a href="/wiki/User:Butlerblog" title="User:Butlerblog"><span style="font-weight:bold;"><span style="color:#333366;">Butler</span><span style="font-style:italic;color:#D2B48C;">Blog</span></span></a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Butlerblog" title="User talk:Butlerblog">talk</a>) 17:25, 31 May 2021 (UTC)
       </dd>
      </dl>

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Page_mover"><span class="anchor" id="rperm-pagemover"></span>Page mover</span></h3> 
      <div class="anonymous-show boilerplate metadata" style="background:#dee; border:1px solid #00c; margin:0.5em; padding:0.5em;; padding: 1em; width:70%">
       Sorry, please be aware that <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:IP" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:IP">unregistered users</a> cannot be granted permissions due to technical restrictions. Please <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ACCOUNT" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:ACCOUNT">create an account</a> in order to request user account permissions.

      <dl>
       <dd>
        I have been regularly moving pages for almost a year and been reviewing articles at AFC for several months. Initially, I was confused about updating links and updating fair use rationales, but I now think I understand the rules enough to apply for this right. The reason I want this right is so that I can move articles on American High Schools without asking other people with this right to do it for me when I cannot perform the move myself. I have read <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PMRC" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:PMRC">WP:PMRC</a> very carefully. In addition to my personal page moves, I have also participated in some page move discussions. If I am unsure if a move is controversial, I will start a discussion and get other peoples' opinions. Again, I promise I will not cause any damage to the project. This is an advanced right that I know requires more care than other rights. I already have a category move in mind that I will do without any objections if I receive this right. Thank you all. <a href="/wiki/User:Scorpions13256" title="User:Scorpions13256">Scorpions13256</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Scorpions13256" title="User talk:Scorpions13256">talk</a>) 17:59, 31 May 2021 (UTC) 
        <dl>
         <dd>
          I'm not seeing a huge need, but the RM and RM/TR displayed mostly matches the end consensus result. Put me down in the weak support / temporary granting camp. <a href="/wiki/User:Primefac" title="User:Primefac">Primefac</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Primefac" title="User talk:Primefac">talk</a>) 13:40, 1 June 2021 (UTC)

           <dd>
            <span class="template-ping">@<a href="/wiki/User:Primefac" title="User:Primefac">Primefac</a>:</span> I see you responded. If it makes a difference, I plan on helping out at RM/TR when I feel I am qualified to determine whether the request is appropriate. <a href="/wiki/User:Scorpions13256" title="User:Scorpions13256">Scorpions13256</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Scorpions13256" title="User talk:Scorpions13256">talk</a>) 23:06, 2 June 2021 (UTC)

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pending_changes_reviewer"><span class="anchor" id="rperm-reviewer"></span>Pending changes reviewer</span></h3> 
      <div class="anonymous-show boilerplate metadata" style="background:#dee; border:1px solid #00c; margin:0.5em; padding:0.5em;; padding: 1em; width:70%">
       Sorry, please be aware that <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:IP" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:IP">unregistered users</a> cannot be granted permissions due to technical restrictions. Please <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ACCOUNT" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:ACCOUNT">create an account</a> in order to request user account permissions.

      <dl>
       <dd>
        I am familiar with Wikipedia's guidance and ruleset, the Mediawiki software, and most importantly how to identify appropriate contributions. I have also <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Wingwatchers" title="Special:Contributions/Wingwatchers">contributed</a> significantly to Wikipedia for the past month. As for the undos, I am sorry for those; one time was I trying to test the Twinkle extension on the mainpage, one time was I tried to replace <a href="/wiki/Safari_(web_browser)" title="Safari (web browser)">Safari</a>'s infobox image from local to Commons, one time was non-constructive. There were also fair use image claims too, beforehand I had no idea Wikipedia is that serious about fair use material than <a href="/wiki/Wookieepedia" title="Wookieepedia">Wookieepedia</a>. I would try my best to avoid those mistakes.<a href="/wiki/User:Wingwatchers" title="User:Wingwatchers">Wingwatchers</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Wingwatchers" title="User talk:Wingwatchers">talk</a>) 02:57, 3 June 2021 (UTC)

      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        Hi. I've been reverting vandalism for quite a while on Wikipedia and have well over the 200 necessary mainspace edits for usage of the tool. I have found that a lot of the time there is vandalism that occurs that happens over multiple edits, and rather than having to go into the last stable version of the article and copy and paste the entire impacted section (as I've had to do for a few articles) it'd be far more helpful to just be able to roll all the vandalism back with the click of a button. Having been involved in reverting a lot of vandalism lately and getting pages protected after this, I've made myself familiar with <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:VAND" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:VAND">WP:VAND</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ROLLBACK" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:ROLLBACK">WP:ROLLBACK</a> and vow to stick rigidly to these guidelines if granted permission. Thanks! <span class="autosigned" style="font-size:85%;">—&nbsp;Preceding <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Signatures" title="Wikipedia:Signatures">unsigned</a> comment added by <a href="/wiki/User:Ser!" title="User:Ser!">Ser!</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ser!#top" title="User talk:Ser!">talk</a> • <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Ser!" title="Special:Contributions/Ser!">contribs</a>) 12:52, 23 May 2021 (UTC)</span>
       </dd>
      </dl>

        I'm requesting rollback rights and permissions after being denied twice due to inexperience in my first year/year and a half of editing on Wikipedia. I believe that I now possess the knowledge and have the experience to be able to utilise rollback rights appropriately after over 1500+ mainspace edits and using Twinkle for almost two years. I understand if you want any questions answered regarding my experience and if any of my activity might seem to be questionable. I believe Huggle would benefit my anti-vandalism efforts. <a href="/wiki/User:KaitoNkmra23" title="User:KaitoNkmra23"><span style="font-family:'Georgia';font-weight:100;text-shadow:2px 2px 10px green;color:green;">KaitoNkmra23</span></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:KaitoNkmra23" title="User talk:KaitoNkmra23"><span style="font-family:'Georgia';text-shadow:2px 2px 10px blue;color:blue;">talk</span></a> 05:10, 26 May 2021 (UTC)

        Hey, I am a recent changes patroller, and I have mostly used Twinkle to revert edits. I have knowledge that rollback should usually only be used for vandalism and other clear reasons, and I can tell the difference between a good faith edit and a bad faith one well. I am applying for rollback to be able to revert vandalism more quickly. <a href="/wiki/User:GameTriangle" title="User:GameTriangle"><span style="background-color:yellow; color:black;"><b>GameTriangle</b></span></a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:GameTriangle" title="User talk:GameTriangle">talk</a>) 21:13, 27 May 2021 (UTC)

       <dd>
        <a href="/wiki/User:Chynapras" title="User:Chynapras">Chynapras</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Chynapras" title="User talk:Chynapras">talk</a>) 18:01, 29 May 2021 (UTC)
       </dd>

      <p>Hello. I am Wikipedia editor Chynapras. Recently, I have been fighting vandalism. I edit a lot these days but didn’t use to edit much before. As I am editing a lot these days, I have been encountering vandalisms as well. I have made well over 870 edits and more than 660 of those edits came from the last 30 days. I think I have become a experienced editor to gain this right. I want to fight vandalism so this right would make it a lot easier for me. If I gain this right, I would fight vandalism even more than I am fighting now. I want to make Wikipedia a place full of accurate grammar and informations removing vandalism. I hope you understand. Thank you. </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>

         <dd>

                        I just took a look through the last couple of hundred contributions you've made. I'm seeing some good content work, and a lot of edits to your user space (which is totally fine when you're learning how to edit, no problem implied there), but I'm not seeing any counter-vandalism work. Twinkle will do almost everything that Rollback does (I go whole months without using the actual Rollback tool, but I use Twinkle every day) - if you want the permission, build up experience using Twinkle, show that you can identify vandalism, revert it appropriately and warn users with the correct templates, then reapply here. <a href="/wiki/User:Girth_Summit" title="User:Girth Summit"><span style="font-family:Impact;color:#006400;">Girth</span><span style="font-family:Impact;color:#4B0082;">Summit</span></a><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Girth_Summit" title="User talk:Girth Summit"><sub style="font-family:Segoe print;color:blue;"> (blether)</sub></a> 06:20, 2 June 2021 (UTC)

      <dl>
       <dd>
        I have made more than 5,000 edits on English Wikipedia, and I've worked on counter vandalism unit many times using twinkle. Is it possible to get the rollback right? <a href="/wiki/User:Tamingimpala" title="User:Tamingimpala">Tame</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Tamingimpala" title="User talk:Tamingimpala">talk</a>) 15:18, 4 June 2021 (UTC)

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Template_editor"><span class="anchor" id="rperm-templateeditor"></span>Template editor</span></h3> 
      <div class="anonymous-show boilerplate metadata" style="background:#dee; border:1px solid #00c; margin:0.5em; padding:0.5em;; padding: 1em; width:70%">
       Sorry, please be aware that <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:IP" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:IP">unregistered users</a> cannot be granted permissions due to technical restrictions. Please <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ACCOUNT" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:ACCOUNT">create an account</a> in order to request user account permissions. 
      </div>
      <div class="user-show"> 
       <dl>
        <dd>
         <dl>
          <dt>
           (<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Template_editor&amp;action=edit&amp;section=new&amp;nosummary=true&amp;preload=Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Template_editor/Preload&amp;preloadparams%5b%5d=template+editor">add request</a> • <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Requests_for_permissions/Template_editor" title="Wikipedia:Requests for permissions/Template editor">view requests</a></span>)
          </dt>
         </dl>
        </dd>
       </dl> 
      </div>

      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="template-ping">@<a href="/wiki/User:Primefac" title="User:Primefac">Primefac</a>:</span> Request for TE renewal. I've made reasonable use of the TE right, answering some edit requests and so on. I have responded where issues have been raised, e.g. <a href="/wiki/Special:PermanentLink/1026347186#Bullet_points" title="Special:PermanentLink/1026347186">Special:Permalink/1026347186#Bullet_points</a>. Old discussion: <a href="/wiki/Special:PermanentLink/1016705537#User:GKFX" title="Special:PermanentLink/1016705537">Special:PermanentLink/1016705537#User:GKFX</a> <a href="/wiki/User:GKFX" title="User:GKFX">User:GKFX</a><sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:GKFX" title="User talk:GKFX">talk</a></sup> 21:25, 5 June 2021 (UTC) 
        <dl>
         <dd>
          <img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/15px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="15" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/23px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Pictogram_voting_comment.svg/30px-Pictogram_voting_comment.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="250" data-file-height="250">&nbsp;<b>Automated comment</b> This user was <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=User:GKFX&amp;type=rights&amp;offset=20210408170015&amp;limit=1">granted</a> temporary template editor rights by <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/User:Primefac">Primefac</a></span> (expires 00:00, 8 July 2021 (UTC)). <span style="font-family:sans-serif">— <b><a href="/wiki/User:MusikBot" title="User:MusikBot"><span style="color:black; font-style:italic">MusikBot</span></a> <sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:MusikAnimal" title="User talk:MusikAnimal"><span style="color:green">talk</span></a></sup></b></span> 21:30, 5 June 2021 (UTC) 
          <dl>
           <dd>
            I'm going to abstain from reviewing this, but I will note <a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Infobox#Semi-serious_question_about_deprecation" title="Template talk:Infobox">this discussion</a> as potentially relevant. <a href="/wiki/User:Primefac" title="User:Primefac">Primefac</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Primefac" title="User talk:Primefac">talk</a>) 21:32, 5 June 2021 (UTC) 
            <dl>
             <dd>
              Yes apologies for the inconvenience caused there. After monitoring <a href="/wiki/Category:Pages_where_post-expand_include_size_is_exceeded" title="Category:Pages where post-expand include size is exceeded">Category:Pages where post-expand include size is exceeded</a> for a while I thought it would be helpful to make a pre-emptive bit of maintenance and use more modules directly, particularly with navboxes and infoboxes, rather than waiting for pages to break. As Izno mentioned there, there had been some discussion broadly in favour of such usage (although not of course for my specific bit of bulk editing) and I thought it seemed like reasonably harmless and uncontroversial cleanup.
             </dd> 
             <dd>
              Re-reading the discussion it does seem to have been mostly the naming that was in dispute. While I get Izno's point that the syntax <code>{{#invoke:Infobox3cols||args...}}</code> might be a bit cryptic, I had specifically set up <a href="/wiki/Module:Infobox3cols" title="Module:Infobox3cols">the doc page</a> to show exactly how to use the module so I do feel that I had done my best there. <a href="/wiki/User:GKFX" title="User:GKFX">User:GKFX</a><sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:GKFX" title="User talk:GKFX">talk</a></sup> 21:54, 5 June 2021 (UTC) 
              <dl>
               <dd>
                For what it's worth, I'm not presenting that as evidence for or against granting, just as something for the reviewing admin to consider. <a href="/wiki/User:Primefac" title="User:Primefac">Primefac</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Primefac" title="User talk:Primefac">talk</a>) 21:57, 5 June 2021 (UTC)
               </dd>
              </dl>
             </dd> 
             <dd>
              I see the naming functions the empty string thing as a good faith thing thought to be uncontroversial and wouldn't hold it against them at all. While I agree it is a bad design choice and was rightly reverted we all make mistakes. The other edits of theirs that I've seen look good, but that's far from comprehensive. --<a href="/wiki/User:Trialpears" title="User:Trialpears">Trialpears</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Trialpears" title="User talk:Trialpears">talk</a>) 22:09, 5 June 2021 (UTC)
             </dd>
            </dl>
           </dd>
          </dl>
         </dd>
        </dl>
       </dd>
      </dl>
